the serenad

hast t stillest hour night
the moon shed palest light
and sleep chain lake hill
the wood plain babbl rill
and yon ivi lattic show
My fair one slumber repos
come ye know love maid
and help prepar serenad
hither night flown
bring instrument everi tone
but lest nois ye wake lull
her dream fanci ye must cull
such shall sooth mind
and leav harshest behind
bring thunder drum yet
the harshlyshriek clarionet
nor scream hautboy trumpet shrill
nor clang cymbal skill
exclud one would disturb
the fairi architect curb
the wild creation mirth
all would wake soul earth
choos ye softlybreathingflut
the mellow horn love lute
the viol must forget
and take sprightli flageolet
and grave bassoon choos fife
whose warbl tune strife
mingl mysteri word
may seem like note blithest bird

are ye prepar now lightli tread
As elfin minstrel led
and fling sound upon air
shall rude wake slumber fair
softli now breath symphoni
So gentli breath tone may vie
In soft magic note
In vision heard music float
So buoyant well may seem
with strain ether dream
one song mysteri birth
she doubt come heaven earth
play My love one slumber still
play she wake thrill
Of joy produc strain mild
but fanci mould gay wild
now music low declin
T sigh forest pine
Or t fit vari war
Of distant fall troubl shore
now tone grow full sharp
T whisper aeolian harp
the viol swell low loud
T spirit chant cloud
that pass It die away
So gentli die scarc say
T gone listen t lost fear
listen think hear
As dew drop mingl stream
To t one bliss dream
A song angel throne light
softli away fair one goodnight
